z'4tf ;'lglZrt u/ fpF5
(Internal controls are the mechanisms, rules, and procedures
implemented by an organization to ensure the integrity of financial and accounting
information, promote accountability and prevent fraud. Besides complying with laws
and regulations and preventing employees from stealing assets or commiting fraud,
.
